This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-kitchen-initial)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry corridor unknown_south - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at pantry)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (door-between kitchen pantry north)
    (door-between pantry kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry north)
    (door-open pantry kitchen south)
    (door-between kitchen unknown_south south)
    (door-closed kitchen unknown_south south)
    ;; No door between kitchen and corridor east as observed in the environment
    ;; No door between kitchen and living room west as observed in the environment
  )
  (:goal
    (at unknown_south)
  )
)

  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))

      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))

      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-kitchen-initial)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry laundry_room corridor living_room - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (explored laundry_room)
    (door-between kitchen pantry north)
    (door-between pantry kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry north)
    (door-open pantry kitchen south)
    (door-between kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-between laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-open laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-between kitchen corridor east)
    (door-between kitchen living_room west)
    (door-closed kitchen corridor east)
    (door-closed kitchen living_room west)
  )
  (:goal
    (at corridor)
  )
)

Generated df and pf: 
 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-kitchen-initial)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry laundry_room corridor - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (explored laundry_room)
    (door-between kitchen pantry north)
    (door-between pantry kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry north)
    (door-open pantry kitchen south)
    (door-between kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-between laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-open laundry_room kitchen north)
  )
  (:goal
    (at corridor)
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-kitchen-initial)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry laundry_room corridor - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (explored laundry_room)
    (door-between kitchen pantry north)
    (door-between pantry kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry north)
    (door-open pantry kitchen south)
    (door-between kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-between laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-open laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-between kitchen corridor east)
    (door-closed kitchen corridor east)
  )
  (:goal
    (at corridor)
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-kitchen-initial)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry laundry_room - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at laundry_room)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (explored laundry_room)
    (door-between kitchen pantry north)
    (door-between pantry kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry north)
    (door-open pantry kitchen south)
    (door-between kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-between laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-open laundry_room kitchen north)
  )
  (:goal
    (at kitchen)
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-kitchen-initial)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry laundry_room corridor living_room - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (explored laundry_room)
    (door-between kitchen pantry north)
    (door-between pantry kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry north)
    (door-open pantry kitchen south)
    (door-between kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-between laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-open laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-between kitchen corridor east)
    (door-between kitchen living_room west)
    ;; unexplored: corridor, living_room
  )
  (:goal
    (or (at corridor) (at living_room))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)


This is previous problem file:

  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry laundry_room corridor - location
    north south east west - direction
  )

    (at kitchen)

    (explored pantry)
    (explored laundry_room)

    (door-between pantry kitchen south)

    (door-open kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-open laundry_room kitchen north)

  )

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-kitchen-progress)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry laundry_room - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at pantry)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (explored laundry_room)
    (door-between kitchen pantry north)
    (door-between pantry kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry north)
    (door-open pantry kitchen south)
    (door-between kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-between laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-open laundry_room kitchen north)
  )
  (:goal
    (at kitchen)
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )

  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)

    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))

    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)

    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))

    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-kitchen-progress)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry laundry_room corridor - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (explored laundry_room)
    (door-between kitchen pantry north)
    (door-between pantry kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry north)
    (door-open pantry kitchen south)
    (door-between kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-between laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-open laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-between kitchen corridor east)
    (door-between corridor kitchen west)
    (door-closed kitchen corridor east)
    (door-closed corridor kitchen west)
  )
  (:goal
    (at corridor)
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous problem file:

  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-kitchen-progress)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry laundry_room - location
    north south - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (explored laundry_room)
    (door-between kitchen pantry north)
    (door-between pantry kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry north)
    (door-open pantry kitchen south)
    (door-between kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-between laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-open laundry_room kitchen north)
  )
  (:goal
    (at pantry)
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )
  
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)

    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )
  
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )
  
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

Generated df and pf: 
 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-kitchen-progress)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry laundry_room corridor living_room - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (explored laundry_room)
    (door-between kitchen pantry north)
    (door-between pantry kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry north)
    (door-open pantry kitchen south)
    (door-between kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-between laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen laundry_room south)
    (door-open laundry_room kitchen north)
    (door-between kitchen corridor east)
    (door-between kitchen living_room west)
  )
  (:goal
    (at corridor)
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)


This is previous problem file:

    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry laundry_room corridor living_room - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (explored laundry_room)
    (door-between kitchen pantry north)
    (door-between pantry kitchen south)

    (door-between kitchen living_room west)
    (door-between living_room kitchen east)
    (door-closed kitchen living_room west)
    (door-closed living_room kitchen east)
  )

  )

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

Generated df and pf: 
 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)
